<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN" ALIGN="CENTER">
<B>
	MARINE PETROLEUM TRUST AND SUBSIDIARY
</B>
</P>
<EFX_NOTES_TO_FINANCIAL_STATEMENT>
<A NAME="FIS_NOTES_TO_FINANCIAL_STATEMENT"></A>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN" ALIGN="CENTER">
<B>
<A NAME="D260739D10K_HTM_TX260739_29">
</A>
	NOTES TO CONSOLIDATED FINANCIAL STATEMENTS
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:12PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
<B>
	(1)
</B>
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
<B>
	Summary of Significant Accounting Policies
</B>
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:6PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
<I>
	(a)
</I>
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
<I>
	General
</I>
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:6PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:8%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	Marine Petroleum Trust (the &#147;Trust&#148;) was established on June&nbsp;1,
	1956 with the transfer of property to the Trust consisting of certain contract rights, units of beneficial interest and common stock in exchange for units of beneficial interest in the Trust. The contract rights entitled the Trust to receive an
	overriding royalty interest in oil, natural gas and other mineral leasehold interests acquired by Gulf Oil Corporation, now Chevron U.S.A., Inc. (&#147;Chevron&#148;), a subsidiary of Chevron Corporation, in certain areas of the Gulf of Mexico prior
	to January&nbsp;1, 1980.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:8%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	The Trust must distribute all income, after paying its liabilities and obligations, to the unitholders during
	the months of March, June, September and December each year. The Trust and its subsidiary cannot engage in a trade or business. Funds held by Marine Petroleum Corporation, a wholly owned subsidiary of the Trust, (&#147;MPC,&#148; and collectively
	with the Trust, &#147;Marine&#148;) pending distribution to the Trust are invested in U.S. Treasury and agency bonds.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:8%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	The unitholders
	assigned their contract rights offshore of Louisiana to MPC reserving a 98% net profits interest to themselves. The net profits interest contract was transferred to the Trust along with the other properties. The Trust is authorized to pay expenses
	of MPC should it be necessary.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:8%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	The Trust is to continue until June&nbsp;1, 2021, or until such later date as holders of the units owning
	a majority of the outstanding units may designate, but in any event, not more than 20 years from such designation. However, the unitholders owning eighty percent (80%)&nbsp;or more of the outstanding units may terminate the Trust on any date.
</P>
<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:12PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
<I>
	(b)
</I>
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
<I>
	Principles of Consolidation
</I>
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:6PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:8%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	The consolidated financial statements include the Trust and
	its wholly owned subsidiary, MPC. All material intercompany accounts and transactions have been eliminated upon consolidation.
</P>
<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:12PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
<I>
	(c)
</I>
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
<I>
	Producing Oil and Gas Properties
</I>
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:6PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:8%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	At the time the Trust was established, no determinable
	market value was available for the assets transferred to the Trust; consequently, nominal values were assigned. Accordingly, no allowance for depletion has been included. All income from oil and natural gas royalties relate to proved developed oil
	and natural gas reserves.
</P>
<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:12PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
<I>
	(d)
</I>
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
<I>
	U.S. Federal Income Taxes
</I>
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:6PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:8%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	No provision has been made for U.S. Federal income taxes on
	the Trust&#146;s income since such taxes are the liability of the unitholders.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:8%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	U.S. Federal income taxes have been provided on the income
	of MPC (which specifically excludes the 98% net profits interest to be retained by and&nbsp;delivered to the Trust), after deducting statutory depletion. MPC uses the cash method of reporting for U.S. Federal income taxes.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:8%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	The primary difference between the actual tax expense of MPC and the expected tax expense is due to the fact that only 2% of MPC&#146;s income
	(i.e., excluding the 98% net profits interest retained by, and delivered to, the Trust) is subject to U.S. Federal income tax.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT ; FONT-SIZE:8PT">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN" ALIGN="CENTER">
	-27-
</P>
<A NAME="eolPage28"></A>
<P STYLE='PAGE-BREAK-BEFORE:ALWAYS'>
<HR SIZE="3" STYLE="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<H5 ALIGN="LEFT">
<A HREF="#D260739D10K_HTM_TOC">
	Table of Contents
</A>
</H5>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:8%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	Tax positions taken by the Trust related to the Trust&#146;s pass-through status and federal
	state tax positions have been reviewed, and the Trustee is of the opinion that material positions taken would more likely than not be sustained upon an examination. In accordance with the Trust&#146;s basis of accounting discussed in Note 2, the
	Trust would only recognize the impact of tax positions that were not upheld at the time of payment. As of June 30, 2016, the Trust&#146;s tax years 2012 through 2015 remain subject to examination.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:8%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	MPC recognizes interest and penalties related to unrecognized tax benefits in income tax expense.
</P>
<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:12PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
<I>
	(e)
</I>
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
<I>
	Credit Risk Concentration and Cash Equivalents
</I>
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:6PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:8%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	Financial instruments which potentially
	subject Marine to concentrations of credit risk are primarily investments in cash equivalents, U.S. Treasury and agency bonds. The Trust and MPC place their cash investments with financial institutions or companies that the Trustee considers credit
	worthy and limit the amount of credit exposure from any one financial institution.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:8%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	Marine had cash and cash equivalents of $817,381 and
	$792,265 at June&nbsp;30, 2016 and 2015, respectively, which consisted of cash deposits, U.S. Treasury and agency bonds and money market accounts.
</P>
<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:12PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
<I>
	(f)
</I>
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
<I>
	Use of Estimates
</I>
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:6PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:8%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	The preparation of financial statements in conformity with the
	modified cash basis method of accounting requires the Trustee to make various estimates and assumptions that affect the reported amount of liabilities at the date of the financial statements and the reported amount of expenses during the reporting
	period.&nbsp;Actual results may differ from such estimates.
</P>
<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:12PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
<I>
	(g)
</I>
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
<I>
	Distributable Income per Unit and Distributions
</I>
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:6PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:8%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	Distributable income per unit is
	determined by dividing distributable income by the number of units of beneficial interest outstanding during the period. Distributions to unitholders are calculated and paid out net of reserve for future expenses, which are estimated by the Trustee
	on a quarterly basis.
</P>
<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:12PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">

	(h)
</I>
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
<I>
	Significant Royalty Sources
</I>
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:6PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:8%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	Percent of royalty revenue received by Marine from
	producers is summarized as follows:
</P>
<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:12PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;

<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:6PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="9%">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
	&#149;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="TOP">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
	Marine&#146;s expenses (which include accounting, legal, and other professional fees, Trustees&#146; fees and out-of-pocket expenses) are recorded on an actual paid basis. Reserves for liabilities that are contingent or
	uncertain in amount may also be established if considered necessary.
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:6PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="9%">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
	&#149;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="TOP">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
	Distributions to unitholders are recognized when declared by the Trustee of the Trust.
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:8%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	The
	financial statements of Marine differ from financial statements prepared in conformity with GAAP because of the following:
</P>
<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:6PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="9%">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
	&#149;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="TOP">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
	Royalty income is recognized in the month received rather than in the month of production.
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:6PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="9%">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
	&#149;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="TOP">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
	Reserves may be established for contingencies that would not be recorded under GAAP.
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:6PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="9%">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
	&#149;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="TOP">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
	Expenses are recorded in the month paid rather than in the month incurred.
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:8%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	This comprehensive
	basis of accounting corresponds to the accounting principles permitted for royalty trusts by the Securities and Exchange Commission (the &#147;SEC&#148;), as specified by Staff Accounting Bulletin Topic 12:E, Financial Statements of Royalty Trusts.
</P>
<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:12PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
<B>
	(3)
</B>
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
<B>
	Investment in Affiliate &#150; Tidelands Royalty Trust &#147;B&#148;
</B>
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:6PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:8%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	At June&nbsp;30,
	2016 and 2015, the Trust owned 32.6% of the outstanding units of beneficial interest in Tidelands Royalty Trust &#147;B&#148; (&#147;Tidelands&#148;). The 452,366 units owned by the Trust had a market value $515,697 and $701,167 at June&nbsp;30,
	2016 and 2015, respectively, based on the closing price of Tideland&#146;s units on the OTC Bulletin Board on such dates.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:8%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	Administrative
	expenses are shared by MPC and Tidelands Royalty Trust &#147;B&#148; Corporation, a wholly owned subsidiary of Tidelands, in the ratio of each of MPC&#146;s and Tidelands Royalty Trust &#147;B&#148; Corporation&#146;s gross oil and natural gas
	royalties to the total gross oil and natural gas royalties of both entities. These administrative expenses were associated with the lease of an office space that terminated as of April&nbsp;30, 2014.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:8%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">

</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
<B>
	(6)
</B>
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
<B>
	Texas Franchise Tax
</B>
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:6PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:8%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	Texas imposes a franchise tax that applies to most business
	entities that are formed or qualified to do business, or which are otherwise doing business, in Texas. Under the Texas franchise tax, a 0.75% tax is imposed for reports due in 2017 on each taxable entity&#146;s taxable margin that is apportioned to
	Texas. Taxable margin is generally defined as revenues less certain costs. Taxable entities include most entities that provide owners with limited liability protection, including trusts. There are certain exemptions from the franchise tax, including
	exclusions for certain &#147;passive entities&#148; that satisfy specified statutory requirements as described below and entities with total revenues below a specified threshold.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:8%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	Under the Texas franchise tax, &#147;passive entities&#148; include trusts that meet the following requirements: (a)&nbsp;the trust cannot be
	a business trust within the meaning of U.S. Treasury Regulation section 301.7701-4(b); (b)&nbsp;at least 90% of the trust&#146;s income for the taxable year must be derived from passive sources (e.g., royalties, bonuses, delay rental income from
	mineral properties, dividends, interest, and gains from the sale of securities); and (c)&nbsp;no more than 10% of the trust&#146;s income for the taxable year can be derived from an active trade or business (e.g., rent, certain income received by a
	non-operator under a joint operating agreement pursuant to which the operator is the member of an affiliated group that includes such non-operator). An entity will determine on an annual basis whether it meets the requirements to be treated as a
	&#147;passive entity&#148; for the Texas franchise tax. The Trustee believes that all or substantially all of the income of the Trust currently is passive, as it consists of royalty income from the sale of oil and natural gas, dividends and interest
	income. Thus, the Trust anticipates that it will be a passive entity in the tax year ending in 2016. Subject to any change in the sources of income derived by the Trust or any change in the Indenture, the Trust expects that it will continue to
	qualify as a passive entity that is not subject to the franchise tax.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:8%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	If the Trust is exempt from the Texas franchise tax as a passive
	entity, each unitholder that is subject to the Texas franchise tax as a taxable entity under the Texas Tax Code should generally include its share of the Trust&#146;s revenue in its franchise tax computation. The Texas franchise tax does not apply
	to natural persons.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:8%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	In the event that the Trust does not qualify as a passive entity, it would not be required to pay any tax and is not
	considered to owe any Texas franchise tax for any period in which its annualized total revenue is less than or equal to a certain threshold. For reports due on or after January&nbsp;1, 2016 and before January&nbsp;1, 2018, this no tax due threshold
	is $1,110,000.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:8%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	Each unitholder is urged to consult its own tax advisor regarding the requirements for filing state tax returns.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT ; FONT-SIZE:8PT">
	&nbsp;

	-31-

<EFX_EXHIBIT_99>
<A NAME="FIS_EXHIBIT_99"></A>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN" ALIGN="RIGHT">
<B>
	Exhibit 99.1
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN" ALIGN="CENTER">
<B>
	REPORT OF INDEPENDENT REGISTERED
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN" ALIGN="CENTER">
<B>
	PUBLIC ACCOUNTING FIRM
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	To the Trustee and
	Stockholders of
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	Tidelands Royalty Trust &#147;B&#148; and subsidiary
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	We have audited the accompanying consolidated statements of assets, liabilities and trust corpus of Tidelands Royalty Trust &#147;B&#148; and Subsidiary (the
	Trust) as of December&nbsp;31, 2015 and 2014, and the related consolidated statements of distributable income and changes in trust corpus for each of the years in the three-year period ended December&nbsp;31, 2015. The Trust&#146;s management is
	responsible for these consolidated financial statements. Our responsibility is to express an opinion on these consolidated financial statements based on our audits.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	We conducted our audits in accordance with the standards of the Public Company Accounting Oversight Board (United States). Those standards require that we
	plan and perform the audit to obtain reasonable assurance about whether the consolidated financial statements are free of material misstatement. The Trust is not required to have, nor were we engaged to perform, an audit of its internal control over
	financial reporting. Our audit included consideration of internal control over financial reporting as a basis for designing audit procedures that are appropriate in the circumstances, but not for the purpose of expressing an opinion on the
	effectiveness of the Trust&#146;s internal control over financial reporting. Accordingly, we express no such opinion. An audit also includes examining, on a test basis, evidence supporting the amounts and disclosures in the consolidated financial
	statements, assessing the accounting principles used and significant estimates made by management, as well as evaluating the overall financial statement presentation. We believe that our audits provide a reasonable basis for our opinion.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	As described in Note 2 to the consolidated financial statements, these consolidated financial statements were prepared on a modified cash basis of accounting,
	which is a comprehensive basis of accounting other than accounting principles generally accepted in the United States of America.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	In our opinion, the
	consolidated financial statements referred to above present fairly, in all material respects, the assets, liabilities, and trust corpus of Tidelands Royalty Trust &#147;B&#148; and Subsidiary as of December&nbsp;31, 2015 and 2014, and distributable
	income and changes in trust corpus for each of the years in the three-year period ended December&nbsp;31, 2015 in conformity with the modified cash basis of accounting described in Note 2 to the consolidated financial statements.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	WEAVER AND TIDWELL, L.L.P

<P STYLE='PAGE-BREAK-BEFORE:ALWAYS'>
<HR SIZE="3" STYLE="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN" ALIGN="CENTER">
<B>
	TIDELANDS ROYALTY TRUST &#147;B&#148; AND SUBSIDIARY
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN" ALIGN="CENTER">
<B>
	NOTES TO CONSOLIDATED FINANCIAL STATEMENTS
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN" ALIGN="CENTER">
<B>
	DECEMBER 31, 2015
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:12PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
<B>
	(1)
</B>
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
<B>
	SUMMARY OF SIGNIFICANT ACCOUNTING POLICIES AND GENERAL
</B>
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:6PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="8%">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
	(a)
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
	General
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:6PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:13%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	Tidelands Royalty Trust &#147;B&#148; (the &#147;Trust&#148;) was established on
	June&nbsp;1, 1954 with a transfer of contract rights to certain properties to the Trust in exchange for units of beneficial interest. The contract rights enable the Trust to receive an interest in any oil, natural gas or other mineral leases
	obtained by Gulf Oil Corporation, now Chevron U.S.A., Inc. (&#147;Chevron&#148;), which is a subsidiary of Chevron Corporation and its assignees in a designated area of the Gulf of Mexico during a 50-year period that expired on April&nbsp;30, 2001.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:13%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	The Trust is required under its Indenture to distribute all income, after paying its liabilities and obligations, to the unitholders
	quarterly. The Trust cannot invest any of its money for any purpose and cannot engage in a trade or business.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:13%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	The Trust&#146;s
	wholly-owned subsidiary, Tidelands Royalty &#147;B&#148; Corporation (&#147;Tidelands Corporation&#148;), holds title to interests in properties that are situated offshore of Louisiana. Ninety-five percent of all oil, natural gas, and other mineral
	royalties collected by this subsidiary are retained by and delivered to the Trust. Tidelands Corporation, like the Trust, is prohibited from engaging in a trade or business and does only those things necessary for the administration and liquidation
	of its properties. The Trust is authorized to pay the expenses of Tidelands Corporation should it be necessary.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:13%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	The Trust and its
	subsidiary have no employees. Tidelands Corporation has entered into an arrangement with Marine Petroleum Corporation (a wholly-owned subsidiary of Marine Petroleum Trust, an affiliate of the Trust) to share certain administrative expenses related
	to the use of office space that was leased through April&nbsp;30, 2014 and to assist the trustee in the administration of the Trust. For the years ended December&nbsp;31, 2015, 2014 and 2013, Tidelands Corporation paid $0, $9,000 and $36,000,
	respectively, to Marine Petroleum Corporation as reimbursement for the use of such office space. At December&nbsp;31, 2015 and 2014, Marine Petroleum Trust owned 32.6% of the Trust&#146;s outstanding units of beneficial interest.
</P>
<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:12PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="8%">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
	(b)
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
	Unitholder Voting Matters
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:6PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:13%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	On March&nbsp;27, 2001, the unitholders of record at the close of
	business on February&nbsp;16, 2001, approved an amendment to the Indenture to extend the term of the Trust to April&nbsp;30, 2021.
</P>
<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:12PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="8%">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
	(c)
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
	Principles of Consolidation
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:6PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:13%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	The consolidated financial statements include the Trust and its
	wholly-owned subsidiary, Tidelands Corporation. All material intercompany accounts and transactions have been eliminated upon consolidation.
</P>
<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:12PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="8%">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
	(d)
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
	Producing Oil and Natural Gas Properties
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:6PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:13%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	At the time the Trust was established, no
	determinable market value was available for the assets transferred to the Trust; consequently, nominal values were assigned. Accordingly, no allowance for depletion has been included.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:13%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	Tidelands&#146; revenues are derived from production payments and overriding royalty interests related to properties located in the Gulf of
	Mexico.
</P>
<A NAME="eolPage40"></A>
<P STYLE='PAGE-BREAK-BEFORE:ALWAYS'>
<HR SIZE="3" STYLE="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="8%">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
	(e)
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
	U.S. Federal Income Taxes
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:6PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:13%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	No provision has been made for U.S. Federal income taxes on the
	Trust&#146;s income&nbsp;since such taxes are the liability of the unitholders.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:13%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	U.S. Federal income taxes are provided on the income of
	Tidelands Corporation (which specifically excludes the 95% net profits interest to be retained by and&nbsp;delivered to the Trust) after deducting statutory depletion. There were no significant deferred tax assets or liabilities as of
	December&nbsp;31, 2015 and 2014. Tidelands Corporation uses the cash method of reporting for Federal income taxes.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:13%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	The primary
	difference between the actual tax expense of Tidelands Corporation and the expected tax expense is due to the fact that only 5% of Tidelands Corporation&#146;s income (i.e., excluding the 95% net profits interest retained by and delivered to the
	Trust) is subject to U.S. Federal income tax.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:13%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	Tax positions taken by the Trust related to the Trust&#146;s pass-through status and
	Federal state tax positions have been reviewed, and the Trustee is of the opinion that material positions taken would more likely than not be sustained by examination. In accordance with the Trust&#146;s basis of accounting discussed in Note 1, the
	Trust would only recognize the impact of tax positions that were not upheld at the time of payment. As of December&nbsp;31, 2015, the Trust&#146;s tax years 2012 and thereafter remain subject to examination.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:13%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	Tidelands Corporation recognizes interest and penalties related to unrecognized tax benefits in income tax expense.
</P>
<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:12PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="8%">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
	(f)
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
	Credit Risk Concentration and Cash Equivalents
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:6PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:13%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	Financial instruments which potentially
	subject the Trust and Tidelands Corporation to concentrations of credit risk are primarily investments in cash equivalents. The Trust and Tidelands Corporation place their cash investments with financial institutions that the Trustee considers
	creditworthy and limit the amount of credit exposure from any one financial institution. The estimated fair values of cash equivalents approximate the carrying values due to the short term nature of these financial instruments.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:13%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	Tidelands had cash and cash equivalents of $579,803 and $777,926 at December&nbsp;31, 2015 and 2014, respectively, which consisted of cash
	deposits, U.S. Treasury and agency bonds, and money market accounts.
</P>
<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:12PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="8%">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
	(g)
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
	Use of Estimates
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:6PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:13%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	The preparation of financial statements in conformity with the modified cash
	basis method of accounting requires the Trustee to make various estimates and assumptions that affect the reported amount of liabilities at the date of the consolidated financial statements and the reported amount of expenses during the reporting
	period.&nbsp;Actual results may differ from such estimates.
</P>
<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:12PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="8%">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
	(h)
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
	Distributable Income per Unit
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:6PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:13%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	Distributable income per unit is determined by dividing
	distributable income by the number of units of beneficial interest outstanding during the period.
</P>
<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:12PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%">
	&nbsp;

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
<B>
	(2)
</B>
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
<B>
	BASIS OF ACCOUNTING
</B>
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:6PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:13%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	The financial statements of Tidelands have been prepared on the
	modified cash basis method and are not intended to present financial position and results of operations in conformity with generally accepted accounting principles in the United States (&#147;GAAP&#148;). Under the modified cash basis method:
</P>
<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:6PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="8%">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
	&#149;
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
	Royalty income is recognized when received by Tidelands.
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:6PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="8%">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
	&#149;
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
	Tidelands&#146; expenses (which include accounting, legal, and other professional fees, trustees&#146; fees and out-of-pocket expenses) are recorded on an actual paid basis. Reserves for liabilities that are contingent
	or uncertain in amount may also be established if considered necessary.
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:6PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="8%">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
	&#149;
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
	Distributions to unitholders are recognized when declared by the Trustee of the Trust.
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:13%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	The
	financial statements of Tidelands differ from financial statements prepared in conformity with GAAP because of the following:
</P>
<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:6PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="8%">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
	&#149;
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
	Royalty income is recognized in the month received rather than in the month of production.
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:6PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="8%">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
	&#149;
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
	Reserves may be established for contingencies that would not be recorded under GAAP.
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:6PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="8%">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
	&#149;
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
	Expenses are recorded in the month paid rather than in the month incurred.
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:13%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	This
	comprehensive basis of accounting corresponds to the accounting principles permitted for royalty trusts by the SEC, as specified by Staff Accounting Bulletin Topic 12:E,
<I>
	Financial Statements of Royalty Trusts
</I>
	.
</P>
<P STYLE="FONT-SIZE:12PT;MARGIN-TOP:0PT;MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN; FONT-SIZE:10PT" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%">
	&nbsp;
</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="TOP" ALIGN="LEFT">
<B>
	(3)
</B>
</TD>
<TD ALIGN="LEFT" VALIGN="TOP">
<B>
	TEXAS FRANCHISE TAX
</B>
</TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:6PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:13%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	Texas imposes a franchise tax that applies to most business
	entities that are formed or qualified to do business, or that are otherwise doing business, in Texas. Under the Texas franchise tax statute, a 0.75% tax (in certain cases not applicable here, the tax rate is 0.475%) is imposed for reports due in
	2016 on each taxable entity&#146;s taxable margin that is apportioned to Texas. Taxable margin is generally defined as revenues less certain costs, as provided under the statute. Most entities that provide owners with limited liability protection,
	including trusts, are considered to be taxable entities for purposes of the Texas franchise tax. The statute provides certain limited exemptions from the tax, including exclusions for certain &#147;passive entities&#148; that satisfy specified
	statutory requirements as described below.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:13%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	Under the Texas franchise tax statute, &#147;passive entities,&#148; including trusts, that
	meet the following requirements, are exempt from the Texas franchise tax: (a)&nbsp;the trust cannot be a business trust within the meaning of U.S. Treasury Regulation section 301.7701-4(b); (b)&nbsp;at least 90% of the trust&#146;s income for the
	taxable year must be derived from passive sources (e.g., royalties, bonuses, delay rental income from mineral properties, dividends, interest, gains from the sale of securities); and (c)&nbsp;no more than 10% of the trust&#146;s income for the
	taxable year can be derived from an active trade or business (e.g., rent, certain income received by a non-operator under a joint operating agreement pursuant to which the operator is the member of an affiliated group that includes such
	non-operator). An entity will determine on an annual basis whether it meets the requirements to be treated as a &#147;passive entity&#148; for Texas franchise tax purposes. The Trustee believes that all or substantially all of the income of the
	Trust currently is passive, as it consists of royalty income from the sale of oil and natural gas, dividends and interest income. Subject to any change in the sources of income derived by the Trust or any change in the Indenture, the Trust expects
	that it will continue to qualify as a passive entity that is not subject to the franchise tax.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:12PT; MARGIN-BOTTOM:0PT; TEXT-INDENT:13%; FONT-SIZE:10PT; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN">
	If the Trust is exempt from the Texas
	franchise tax as a passive entity, each unitholder that is subject to the Texas franchise tax as a taxable entity under the Texas Tax Code should generally include its share of the Trust&#146;s revenue in its franchise tax computation. The Texas
	franchise tax does not apply to natural persons. The Trust anticipates that it will be a passive entity in the tax year ending in 2015.
</P>
